 ham afsapa ke khilaaf aawaaj uthaaenge

 We have differences among ourselves
 lekin is desh ko bachaane or is desh ke samvidhan ko bachaane main hamaare koi matbhed nahin he

 sena ke khilaaf bayaanbaji par police main shikayatamaamle main bijepi kii yuva ikai (bijevyem) ne police main shikaayat daakhil kar aarope lagaaya he ki kanhaiya ne phir desh virdohi bayaanbaji kar apni jamaanat kii sharton kii andekhi kii he

 desh virdohi narebaaji maamle main he aaropeebataa den ki sansad hamale ke doshi afjal guru kii faansee kaa virodh karne ke liye jeenyu main nau farvari ko ek kaarykram kaa aayojan kiya gaya tha

 While he was allegedly attacked by lawyers during his appearance in Patiala House Court
 akhil bhartiya ayurvigyaan santhaan (ames) santhaan main pichley kuch dinon se jindagi or maut se jujh rahi do saal kii bacchee falak kii haalat guuruuvaar ko bhi najuk bani rahi
 At the same time, the police made a fourth arrest in the case
 ames trama centre ke pramukh emasi mishra ne bataaya, "falak kii haalat gambhir he
 We will remove him from life-saving equipment for some time and see if his organs can work without it
 " Mishra said, "if Falak's condition remains normal without life-saving equipment, it will definitely be a sign of improvement in her health
 antibiotic dawa dene ke baad se bacchee ke fefde ke sankraman main kami ai he
 "it is noteworthy that Falak is suffering from chest, brain and blood transfusions
 use tub ke jariye dawa di ja rahi he
 Mishra said, "our main concern is septicemia (blood transfusion)
 ham uski har ghadi najar rakh rahe hai

 " is bich, falak ko aspataal pahunchane vaali 14 varshiya ladki ko veshyavriti main dhakelne vaali aarti naam kii mahila ko giraftaar kiya gaya he

 tippaniyan Additional Commissioner of Police Ajay Chaudhary said, “aarti will be kept in police custody for three days
 poochtacha ke dauraan usne bataaya ki vah kuch dinon se munarika main kiraye ke ek makaan main rah rahi thi

 " aarti giraftaar duusari mahila puja kii sahyogi he

 jitendra par kishori ko shaareerik rup se pratadit karne kaa aarope he

 bacchee kaa sir phuta hua tha or mastishk main dayee ore khun jam gaya tha

 is kishori ne khud ko bacchee kii maa bataaya tha

 1) For the first time in the history of cricket, the day-night Test was played in Adelaide, Australia
 is match ko dekhne pehle din 47,441 darshak, duusare din 42,372 darshak, tisare din 33,923 darshak aae
 That is, a total of 1,23,736 spectators watched the match on all three days
 2) vaise to cricket kaa janm england main hua, lekin cricket ke sabhi formet kaa pehla match australia ne jeeta he
 Australia defeated England by 45 runs in the first Test match played in 1877
 pehla vanade 1971 australia or england ke bich khelaa gaya
 It was also won by the Kangaroo team by 5 runs
 pehla de-nite vanade bhi australia ke khate main gaya
 In this match, Australia defeated the West Indies by 5 wickets
 agar T20 match kii baat karen to ye bhi pehali baar australia ne jeeta he
 The Kangaroo team defeated New Zealand in this match by 44 runs
 ab pehle de-nite test main bhi australia vijayi rahaa
 Here Kiwis were defeated by Kiwis by 3 wickets
 3) pehla de-nite vanade match 27 november 1979 ko australia ke sidney main khelaa gaya tha
 The first day-night test match this year also started on 27 November
 4) edilade main australia ne 3 wicket se test jeeta or series 2-0 se jiti
 With this win Australia reached number two in the ICC Test rankings
 5) newzealand kii team 2013 ke baad pehali baar koi test series haari he
 During this time the Kiwi team won four series and played three series draws
 aakiri baar england ne kiwi team ko 2013 main 2-0 se test series main haraaya tha
 6) Not a single batsman scored a century in the Adelaide day-night Test between Australia and New Zealand
 isse pehle 1993 main isi maidan par west indies or australia ke hue test match main koi shatak nahin laga tha
 Richie Richardson was the highest scorer in the match, scoring 72 runs
 7) is test main sarvaadhik 66 ran kaa score wicketiper peter navy ne banaaya
 This is the lowest score by any batsman on the Adelaide ground
 isse pehle 1951 main west indies ke kilaaf australia ke dag ring ne 67 ran banaae the
 8) Australia's Josh Hazlewood took 6 wickets for 70 runs in the third innings of the Test and took a total of 9 wickets for 136 runs in the Test
 hezalwood kaa ye test main behtareen pradarshan he
 The comments 9) edilade main pichley 64 saal main pehali baar koi test teen din main khatm hua he
 Earlier in 1951, the West Indies beat Australia by 6 wickets in three days on the same ground
 us match main australia ne toss jitkar pehle ballebaazi kii thi or match haar gai
 This time New Zealand won the toss and elected to bat and lost the match
 10) bharat or dakshin africa ke bich khelaa gaya nagpur test bhi teen din main khatm ho gaya
 Total 247 in this match
 5 over main 652 ran bane or 40 wicket gire
 The Adelaide day-night Test also ended in three days
 is match main 251
 821 runs in 2 overs and total 37 wickets fell
